Action.c(64):     \n
Action.c(64):     function isRadio(formObj) {\n
Action.c(64):       for (j=0; j<formObj.length; j++) {\n
Action.c(64):         if (formObj[j].checked) {\n
Action.c(64):           return true;\n
Action.c(64):         }\n
Action.c(64):       }\n
Action.c(64):       return false;\n
Action.c(64):     }\n
Action.c(64):     \n
Action.c(64):     function isCheck(formObj, form, begin, num) {\n
Action.c(64):       for (j=begin; j<begin+num; j++) {\n
Action.c(64):         if (form.elements[j].checked) {\n
Action.c(64):           return true;\n
Action.c(64):         }\n
Action.c(64):       }\n
Action.c(64):       return false;\n
Action.c(64):     }\n
Action.c(64):     \n
Action.c(64):     function isEmail(str) {\n
Action.c(64):       return ((str != "") && (str.indexOf("@") != -1) && (str.indexOf(".") != -1));\n
